<userid>111832993263988652354<//userid>< Name>
K. A.</Name>
<date>1467477624532< /date>< rating>
5<//rating>
< Text>
The staff is very polite! Very accommodating. Very nice to kids. They really communicate and establish good relationships with their customers. If you are a returning customer they will greet you like they haven't seen you in forever!

They keep the restaurant very clean. There's classy music too so the environment inside is not nauseating.

Keep in mind that since this is a Japanese restaurant expect it to be a little costly. But the food is great! The food's presentation is great! They put a lot in your plate to the point that you can't finish the whole thing so you really get what you paid for.

They have a lot of items in their menu...some of the items' names are even humorous!

They serve salad with sweet salad dressing and it's good. A salad hater might like it. (Like me) I usually order the Pork Katsu and it's delicious! It's not bland at all. The breading is tasty and crispy and they put lots of pieces of it in your plate. Try everything with sauce. The sauce really makes a difference in your food.

P.S.
The tempura ice cream is the best! =) Just ask them about the ice cream once you're ready for dessert! (I think they do this because they deep-fry the ice cream. I think they wanna make sure the ice cream won't melt before they serve it to you)</Text>

< review>
This place started out as a food service truck and now has a restaurant location. I'm sad to say I never had the opportunity to eat from the truck but I'm so glad they now have a restaurant in Cottonwood. Their restaurant location is on front street and not Olive st(I think Olive st was the truck location).

I  have never been more impressed with the food then I was today when I first eat there. I got a few tacos but my favorite was the buffalo chicken taco. It sounded so different that I almost didnt get it but man I'm I glad I did. I'm telling everyone about this place and can't wait to go back and try more new taco flavors. Everyone need to try this place.< /review>

<review>Wow. I usually don't leave bad reviews instead I just don't review it. If you don't have anything nice to say, say nothing. But I am making an exception to this place. I don't know were the high star reviews came from. We were looking for a place to eat after a morning at the beach with the family, and saw the high star reviews and decided to try it. It was a very bad experience. Despite there being only two tables of less than three people and us a party of six with three front house people everything took forever. While we waited to order after having asked for drinks, two other tables came in and left after minutes of just sitting. First red flag. There was a couple sitting next to us that appeared to have finished their queso fundido long ago, when their food arrived. The gentleman just had a bite of his beef tacos and stopped eating, although his companion just stuck to finishing the plate quickly - we at the time assumed he didn't have a big appetite. Second red flag. By this time we had waited 10 minutes to order after having gotten our aguas frescas. The menu items looked promising albeit pricey for common Mexican food -not high dinning. As soon as we ordered the couple next to us asked for their check, it took 15 minutes for the check to arrive, by then we knew we had made a mistake to stick around. We waited 45 for our food and even asked since the other table had just recieved theirs. As soon as we asked about the delay our food started to come in person by person. First dish on the table were the chicken taquitos. The chicken mole taquitos were cold, the sauce watery, and the chicken in them barely had any mole we even asked what had happened to the mole -in their defense they brought us a side of mole. Minutes later, the Guadalajara tacos  made their appearance on the table. The meat was over cooked and didn't taste like Mexican seasoning, although the presentation was great and portions were a decent size. However, the biggest faux paus was that the tortillas for the tacos took minutes to arrive so rice and beans were eaten first. We had asked for three orders of tacos  but only got tortillas for two orders so one person had to wait extra time. When we asked about the whereabouts of the third order we were told they were out. And we had to wait for more to be made. Lastly the mole came in, which was watery and tasted store bought only enhanced with a stick of cinnamon in the process. The meal was overpriced for the quality and time we waited, around 20 dollars per plate. I have had better tasting, authentic, and faster Mexican food out of food trucks in Oakland or San Francisco for half the price. During the entire time we never got asked for a refill on our drinks and we dared not asked for fear of waiting 15 minutes for it. I am a person who has been around the restaurant business for decades, and do not mind the wait or price if service and food are of quality. However, this place didn't have the service or quality. The only thing I can say is that the presentation of some of their plates is great, and their tortillas are hand made and good quality. As we were leaving the lady who makes the tortillas set up shop and was making the tortillas to the public by the window. It was cool to see that and that is why I give them a star.</review><Pictures>None</Pictures>< response>

< Text>
This is such a great little hole-in-the-wall. It's in Downtown Alum Rock (I think), and is never crowded. It has such a chill environment. TVs were playing the World Cup as well as baseball when we went. I ordered the nopale scrambled eggs with fried potato discs, as well as a fish taco, and my boyfriend ordered the pozole with corn tortillas. Both dishes were DELICIOUS. My eggs were busting with cactus pieces, and the flavor was so savory and cactus-y. The fish taco was delectable; the fish pieces were extremely tender and juicy, and seasoned perfectly. Bonus points for having fresh avocado slices!!

My boyfriend was sweating from the heat of his pozole, but still couldn't stop stuffing his face with the bright red soupy goodness in front of him. Service was friendly and quick as well.

I highly recommend this place!!!<//Text>

<Text>Took my Mom and a friend to Sunday breakfast at Linda's. The small but comfortable restaurant  was brightly painted with decorated walls and big televisions to watch the Giants play while we ate. The service was great. It felt as if we were eating at a friend's place. Smiles and friendly greetings when we arrived.
The chips were hard and thick. The salsa was of a mild to medium heat. Nice to taste the individual ingredients as opposed to just hot and burning. Mom  and her friend both order Bacon and Eggs, which they reported " really good bacon", eggs cooked just as ordered,  potatoes in thick round slices, tasty refried beans and good flour tortillas. They were happy with their meals and kept talking about the good sliced potatoes.
I had the Menudo. It was a large bowl with plenty of tripe, and very good broth. It was served with lemon wedges, chopped onion, dried Chile's, oregano and flour tortillas. I asked for cilantro, and it was promptly delivered. I would definitely order the menudo again.
Try Linda's for a  wonderful meal, in a casual and friendly atmosphere, at a reasonable price.< /Text><pictures>None< /pictures>< resp>

[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPcBp5KDbiS9fr4xQXtjUvd2sPNZw5GM1_83uk8=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>
<text>This review is solely based on the service and food quality out of the food truck.
I haven't been inside their restaurant as it's closed for the inside portion during this whole thing going on.

I'm greeted immediately when I walk up to the window. They take my order quality.
The food comes out in a timely manner, can't complain.

With that said let's move onto the food!

I've tried almost everything on the menu but the desserts.

Ribs. seasoned well. Smoked to perfection. Falls off the bone. Great flavor and cooked well. I'd say this alone is worth going for. Especially with the spicy bbq sauce.

Hot links. Spicy and grilled well. These are good with the none spicy bbq sauce since the hot links are already spicy. Perfect balance with the normal sauce.

Mac & cheese. SO good true homemade style Mac N' Cheese. What there to not like about that?

Baked bbq beans. Dip it with their garlic bread and you're in for a treat to the taste buds. And to the stomach. I may have indulged a bit to much of the bread and beans. May have gained some weight LOL.

Coleslaw. Sweet and savory yet refreshing. Especially while eating some heavy bbq meats.

Pulled pork. Savory moist smoked seasoned to perfection. If you like pulled pork sandwiches. I without a doubt know you'll enjoy this.

Would I recommend this place? Most definitely.
For the quality and quantity of food the prices are MORE then fair. This is true BBQ.
Plus the staff is quick and extremely nice.

The only reason I didn't give them 5 stars isn't entirely their fault but still how I do my grading.

Food quality
Food pricing
Service

Decor ( almost deducted another star from this. But I didn't due to the food truck being displayed very well and the menu being very clear )

Cleanliness ( since they're outside using their food truck I couldn't comment on how I give my 5th star ) so there you have it. I hope that this is understandable.

Food: above average

Decor: N/A it's out of their food truck at the moment in the back.

Customer service: no issues at all. Fast and professional service.

Bathrooms. N/A<//text>< user_name>
Lord Van Cannon<//user_name>

<Rate>5< /Rate><review>I went here with my dad to get some food last weekend. There is a catering truck outside where you order food. They have indoor facilities where they prepare the food. When we went there were outdoor tables to sit at in a very open area all adequately spaced for Covid concerns.

We ordered a meat plate that came with two sides and cornbread (you could get a roll if you want). You get your choice of meats and we ordered brisket, spare ribs, and chicken with cornbread. For the sides we had collard greens and mac & cheese. It cost $22 and was quite filling for two people.

The meats were all cooked perfectly and tasted good even without sauce. We got their spicy bbq sauce to go with and it was excellent. The chicken breast was juicy which takes skill to do on the grill.

The mac & cheese and cornbread were solid. And the collard greens were delicious. I will definitely be hitting up this place again.< /review><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< resp>

<Review>Steven, my stylist for eleven years and my colorist for the last three, is brilliant. In all this time, he has consistently delivered the perfect style and color.

Steven patiently talks me through various options, and will offer opinions or follow instructions, or do some combination of both - whatever I ask. I feel safe in his hands because I trust his judgment and impeccable sense of style. He is exceptionally creative and precise.

Steven has executed every kind of hairstyle imaginable with me, at all lengths, as well as highlights of various shades and dimensions. He has done a phenomenal job with both cut and color every time. People always ask me where I get my hair done because he is so awesome.

Of less obvious import, but essential to me, is Steven's presence. He is a smart, hilarious, and kind person. I know for a fact that he won't talk to you if you prefer to sit in the chair in silence, but I never want that. I have fun at my appointments because I get to talk to a high quality person. I can't imagine going to anyone else.

In its current incarnation, Veer & Wander has been around for just a few years, but I didn't notice any turnover when it changed names. As far as I know, they only added people, all of whom I like.

The cosmetics counter came in with the name change. I love it. The people on that side have great ideas, and have taken time trying different products on my face to see what works. I really like shopping in there.

Every experience in my decade there has been positive. That's a rare statement to make with any business relationship, and especially one in a service industry focused on the loaded issue of hair.<//Review>< username>

< Review>
I just rented a storage unit from the Extra Space Storage at 1520 Willow, where Felix is the manager and his wife, Rene, is also working there.

After I reserved a storage unit online, I received a confirmation via email right away and also a reminder of the date. My first impression about this facility when I first got to the office was that Felix welcomed me with a smile and explained everything very clear to me and set up my account. He showed the unit, the floor plan and ways to access my unit.

I drove a couples of times to bring my stuffs to the unit. Every time I was there, I usually saw Felix checking and maintaining the facility and his wife cleaning the place. No wonder the facility always looks clean and neat.

At one time, I had to go to my unit late at night (around 9 pm) and I expressed my concern about the safety at night, both Felix and Rene assured me that the place was safe and informed me that the police station was on the opposite of the road. The information did help me feel better.

Since I just moved to the area, they also gave very useful information regarding where to visit, have good food, or donate some stuffs.

Felix and Rene, thank you for being so helpful and keeping the facility clean.<//Review>

<Review>Rented a 10x20 unit for 16 months to store full household of furniture. Location is fairly convenient relative to major roads. They raised prices three times during the 16 months, ended with $571/month. Front desk is fairly helpful but we didn't ask much of them so can't give assessment there. Besides being extremely expensive, it was a good experience for the first 12 moths...

When I recently returned to the unit to move out, I discovered rats or mice had laid droppings everywhere. While our stuff was well-packed and we incurred very little permanent damage, the extent of contamination was ridiculous. Once we moved everything out, the entire floor was covered in droppings. I also noticed large rodent traps around the entire facility that weren't there before, so I am assuming this a new development.

When I brought this up to management, the head lady at the front desk did not take responsibility for the issue, and suggested that we likely caused the infestation due to food items stored in the unit. We have never stored food items in the unit. This is a property-wide issue at this facility and it's awful. The fact that the local management doesn't want to own it is unfortunate for the Extra Space brand at large, and we let corporate know.

Before you consider storing anything of value here, make sure you review the contractual terms to ensure the facility assumes liability for rodent infestation.
